2/**
3Type aliases for many constants.
4
5This file is generated by typenum's build script.
6
7For unsigned integers, the format is `U` followed by the number. We define aliases for
8
9- Numbers 0 through 1024
10- Powers of 2 below `u64::MAX`
11- Powers of 10 below `u64::MAX`
12
13These alias definitions look like this:
14
15```rust
16use typenum::{B0, B1, UInt, UTerm};
17
18# #[allow(dead_code)]
19type U6 = UInt<UInt<UInt<UTerm, B1>, B1>, B0>;
20```
21
22For positive signed integers, the format is `P` followed by the number and for negative
23signed integers it is `N` followed by the number. For the signed integer zero, we use
24`Z0`. We define aliases for
25
26- Numbers -1024 through 1024
27- Powers of 2 between `i64::MIN` and `i64::MAX`
28- Powers of 10 between `i64::MIN` and `i64::MAX`
29
30These alias definitions look like this:
31
32```rust
33use typenum::{B0, B1, UInt, UTerm, PInt, NInt};
34
35# #[allow(dead_code)]
36type P6 = PInt<UInt<UInt<UInt<UTerm, B1>, B1>, B0>>;
37# #[allow(dead_code)]
38type N6 = NInt<UInt<UInt<UInt<UTerm, B1>, B1>, B0>>;
39```
40
41# Example
42```rust
43# #[allow(unused_imports)]
44use typenum::{U0, U1, U2, U3, U4, U5, U6};
45# #[allow(unused_imports)]
46use typenum::{N3, N2, N1, Z0, P1, P2, P3};
47# #[allow(unused_imports)]
48use typenum::{U774, N17, N10000, P1024, P4096};
49```
50
51We also define the aliases `False` and `True` for `B0` and `B1`, respectively.
52*/
53#[allow(missing_docs)]
54pub mod consts {
55    use crate::uint::{UInt, UTerm};
